/type/author	/authors/OL904150A	6	2017-03-31T10:21:23.827296	{"bio": "[Alexander Bogdanov][1] was a Russian physician, philosopher, science fiction writer, and revolutionary of Belarusian ethnicity.\r\nHe was a key figure in the early history of the Bolshevik faction of the Russian Social Democratic Labor Party, being one of its cofounders and a rival to Vladimir Lenin until being expelled in 1909. In the first decade of the Soviet Union, he was an influential opponent of the government from a Marxist perspective. The polymath Bogdanov received training in medicine and psychiatry. His scientific interests ranged from the universal systems theory to the possibility of human rejuvenation through blood transfusion. He invented an original philosophy called \u201ctectology,\u201d now regarded as a forerunner of systems theory.
